<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wade%E2%80%93Giles" class="extiw" title="w:Wade–Giles">Wade–Giles</a> romanization <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandarin_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Mandarin Chinese"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarin.html>Mandarin</a></a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh">氣</span>／<span class="Hani" lang="zh">气</span> (<i><span class="tr Latn">qì</span></i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Chinese"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chinese.html>Chinese</a></a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh">氣</span> (<i><span class="tr Latn"><span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Old Chinese">OC</span> *kʰɯds</span></i>, “breath, vapor”). <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:modern.html>modern</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language"><a href = vnd.unilang:japanese.html>Japanese</a></a></span> <span class="Jpan" lang="ja"><ruby>気<rp>(</rp><rt>き</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="tr"><span class="mention-tr tr"><a href = vnd.unilang:ki.html>ki</a></span></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Korean_language" class="extiw" title="w:Korean language"><a href = vnd.unilang:korean.html>Korean</a></a></span> <span lang="ko" class="Kore">기</span> (<span lang="ko" class="Kore">氣</span>, <span lang="ko-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:gi.html>gi</a></span>) <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vietnamese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Vietnamese language">Vietnamese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vi">khí</i> (<i class="Hani mention" lang="vi">氣</i>).
</p>
